\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Defines the configuration of all components on the \doxylink{class_c_a_n}{CAN} network.

\Hypertarget{_c_a_n___config_8hpp_a68de8ef23b51dead982cee83e780cf4e}\index{CAN\_Config.hpp@{CAN\_Config.hpp}!CAN\_Map@{CAN\_Map}}
\index{CAN\_Map@{CAN\_Map}!CAN\_Config.hpp@{CAN\_Config.hpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CAN\_Map}{CAN\_Map}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_c_a_n___config_8hpp_a68de8ef23b51dead982cee83e780cf4e} 
etl\+::map CAN\+\_\+\+Map\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Define the \doxylink{class_c_a_n}{CAN} hashmap for all the signals over the \doxylink{class_c_a_n}{CAN} bus network. 

Within the map we will store the Message ID\textquotesingle{}s, and their make up.

For Example; etl\+::pair\{VCU\+\_\+\+PDM\+\_\+\+REAR\+\_\+\+CMD, etl\+::vector$<$\+CAN\+\_\+\+Signal\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, 16$>$

Stores the Key = VCU\+\_\+\+PDM\+\_\+\+REAR\+\_\+\+CMD = 2012 and the Value is a Vector with pointers to the \doxylink{class_c_a_n___signal}{CAN\+\_\+\+Signal} objects Value = \{ \&HSD1\+\_\+\+ID2012, \&HSD2\+\_\+\+ID2012,.....\} the 16 is the number of \doxylink{class_c_a_n}{CAN} signals that can be stored in each message, this has nothing to do with the length of each signal. Each signal defines its bit layout within the message (e.\+g., HSD1\+\_\+\+ID2012\{true, 0, 8\}) so that the message can be correctly packed or unpacked.
